# Wiki Index

The catalog of all pages in this wiki. Each entry: a wikilink to the page and a one-line summary. The LLM reads this first when answering queries to identify candidate pages.

Keep summaries tight ‚Äî one line each. The index is engineered to be cheap to read; a fat index defeats its purpose.

When this file exceeds ~300 lines or the wiki passes ~150 pages, shard into `wiki/indexes/<type>.md` and replace this file with a directory of shards. See the `scaling-playbook.md` reference in the `llm-wiki` skill for the migration procedure.

---

- [[mcp-plan]] ‚Äî the SUPERSEDED (2026-07-01) MCP design doc (sibling of the checklist): v3‚Üív4 rationale, full 241-tool inventory across 12 servers, and the still-valid standards (naming, JSON-Schema 2020-12, error ranges, SemVer, 2-tests-per-tool, doc contract).
- [[mcp-prompt]] ‚Äî the CURRENT one-tool-per-session MCP-completion subagent prompt: names the real 11 servers (server‚Üíproject‚Üífile), the 3-part tool DoD (binding+tests+docs), and reverses the old no-business-asserts test policy. Ground truth: `docs/mcp/MCP_STATUS.md`.

- [[codon-opt-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-OPT-001 (codon optimization / OptimizeSequence): Wikipedia codon-usage-bias + CAI + Plotkin-Kudla 2011 + Mignon 2018 + Kazusa sources; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondary), protein-preservation + Met/Trp-fixed + CAI‚àà(0,1] invariants, E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon tables; RNA-notation + T‚ÜíU + trim-to-codon + 1e-6 CAI clamp implementation notes; no source contradictions.

- [[codon-stats-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-STATS-001 (Codon Usage Statistics, GetStatistics + CalculateCai): the codon-family aggregation/reporting view; bundles RSCU + ENC + CAI + positional GC (GC1/GC2/GC3, GC3s=synonymous-3rd-position GC excluding Met/Trp/stop, Peden 1999) + E. coli/human reference tables; Sharp & Li 1987 + Biopython + Kazusa + CodonW/EMBOSS sources; ATGGCA‚ÜíGC3s 0/GC3 50 + GCTGCC‚ÜíCAI ‚àö0.122 oracles; deviations = GC3s-as-percentage + skip-zero-w (not 0.01 floor); reuses existing codon concepts, no new concept.
- [[codon-usage-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-USAGE-001 (raw codon usage table + TVD comparison, CalculateCodonUsage + CompareCodonUsage): Wikipedia codon-usage-bias + Kazusa + Sharp & Li 1987 sources; unnormalized Dictionary<codon,int> counts (T‚ÜíU, drop partial codon), Similarity=1‚àíŒ£|f‚ÇÅ‚àíf‚ÇÇ|/2 TVD in [0,1] with proven identity/symmetry/range/disjoint‚Üí0 properties, AUGGCUGCU‚Üí{AUG:1,GCU:2} + sim oracles (2/3, 0.5, 0.75, 0.25, disjoint‚Üí0); TVD-not-cosine + empty‚Üí0 deviations; new codon-usage-comparison concept, reuses RSCU counting.
- [[codon-rare-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-RARE-001 (rare codon detection, FindRareCodons + %MinMax/Sherlocc cluster addendum): Wikipedia + GenScript GenRCA (Fan 2024) + Kazusa + Shu 2006 (5√óCUA ~3-fold inhibition) + Sharp & Li 1987 sources; freq<threshold (default 0.15) per-family rule, E. coli AGA/AGG/CGA/CUA rare set; Clarke&Clark 2008 %MinMax 18-codon window (%Min/%Max signed, ¬±100%) + Chartier 2012 Sherlocc 7-codon ‚â•4-slow cluster rule; Arg-family %MinMax oracles (‚àí86.36/+100/+36.47) + Sherlocc 7√óAGA/4+3/3+4 oracles; single-codon-AA no-NaN + overlapping-window-merge corner cases; no contradictions.
- [[compgen-ani-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-ANI-001 (Average Nucleotide Identity, ANIb; first Comparative-genomics file): Goris 2007 + Konstantinidis & Tiedje 2005 + pyani sources; 1020 nt query fragmentation, best-match placement, >30% identity / ‚â•70% alignable cut-offs recalculated over query-fragment length, mean of qualifying fragments; ANI‚âà95%‚Üî70% DDH species boundary; gapped Smith-Waterman recovers indels (AAAACCCC/AAAATCCCC 0.875‚Üí1.0), reciprocal ANI = mean of both directions; exact-arithmetic oracles (1.0/0.9375/0.875, cut-off/short‚Üíexclude‚Üí0); engine decision = LocalAlign not NCBI-BLASTN; deviations None.
- [[compgen-cluster-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-CLUSTER-001 (Conserved Gene Clusters / common intervals of permutations; Comparative-genomics): Uno & Yagiura 2000 + Heber & Stoye 2001 + Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 + Didier et al. 2013 sources; cluster = gene-label set contiguous in EVERY genome (order/strand-free), size ‚â•2, whole set trivial, K‚â•2; golden vector Id‚Çá vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) ‚Üí {1,2}{1,2,3}{3,4,5,6}{4,5}{4,5,6}{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, sequence-with-duplicates {1,2,3,4}; strict gap-free model (maxGap inert, API back-compat only; gene-teams not implemented); deviations None.
- [[compgen-dotplot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001 (Dot Plot Generation, word-match / k-tuple dot matrix; Comparative-genomics): Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 + EMBOSS `dottup` + Wikipedia + Huttley sources; dot at (x,y) iff length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences), `wordSize` (default 10) noise/sensitivity trade-off, `stepSize` x-subsampling; AGCGT/AT k=1‚Üí{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4‚Üí7-dot overlapping set, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjoint‚Üíno dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[compgen-ortho-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-ORTHO-001 (ortholog detection by Reciprocal Best Hits + in-paralog within-genome best hits; Comparative-genomics): Fitch 1970 (orthology=speciation / paralogy=duplication) + Tatusov 1997 (COG symmetrical best hits) + Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 (operational RBH, best hit=max similarity, ‚â•50% coverage, E‚â§1e-6) + Remm 2001 (InParanoid RBH seed + in-paralog rule) sources; RBH reciprocity guard (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog), within-genome mutual best hits = recent paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog/empty oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking; deviations None. Shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, sub-unit of genome-comparison-core-dispensable.
- [[compgen-compare-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-COMPARE-001 (end-to-end genome comparison `CompareGenomes`; Comparative-genomics orchestrating pipeline): Tettelin 2005 (pan-genome core/dispensable) + Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008/Tatusov 1997 (RBH = shared gene) + fraction-of-syntenic-genes metric + MCScanX (Wang 2012) sources; core=RBH ortholog pairs, dispensable=rest, outputs Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped ‚â§1; oracles one-shared‚Üí1/1/1, disjoint‚Üí0/2/2, identical 5-collinear+1‚Üí5/1/1 & 0.8333; symmetric partition; empty‚Üíall-0; two assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate inherited from COMPGEN-RBH-001, MCScanX ‚â•5-anchor block threshold ‚Üí OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[compgen-rearr-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REARR-001 (genome rearrangement detection by breakpoints, signed gene-order comparison; Comparative-genomics): Hunter Lecture 16 (Hannenhalli‚ÄìPevzner/Bafna‚ÄìPevzner) + Tannier PMC3887456 + Bafna‚ÄìPevzner 1998 sources; signed permutation `Œ±(i)=¬±a`, extended `(0,‚Ä¶,n+1)`, breakpoint = pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(‚àíy,‚àíx)` in Œ≤, `b(Œ±)` count + `d_BP=n‚àísim` + reversal lower bound `d‚â•b/2`; Inversion (sign-flip reversal) vs Transposition (orientation-preserving block move); Hunter `Œ±=(‚àí2,‚àí3,+1,+6,‚àí5,‚àí4)`‚Üíb=6, identity‚Üí0, single-inversion‚Üí2 oracles; three scoping assumptions (orthologMap-supplied anchors, strand=sign, only Inversion/Transposition classified ‚Äî Translocation/indel/dup "Not implemented"); the signed-permutation alternative to block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]]; deviations None.
- [[compgen-reversal-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001 (Reversal/inversion distance as the breakpoint lower bound ‚åàb/2‚åâ; Comparative-genomics): NOT a new algorithm ‚Äî the UNSIGNED specialization of [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]'s reversal-distance bound (Bafna‚ÄìPevzner 1998 + Hunter Lecture 16 + H√ºbotter 2020 + Bergeron‚ÄìMixtacki‚ÄìStoye 2009); `CalculateReversalDistance` counts unsigned breakpoints `|Œî|‚âÝ1` on the extended perm and returns `‚åàb/2‚åâ=(b+1)/2`; [2,3,1,6,5,4]‚Üí2, [4,3,2,1]‚Üí1, identity‚Üí0 oracles; lower-bound-not-exact (no HP cycle/hurdle refinement); two assumptions (integer ‚åàb/2‚åâ rounding, unequal-length‚ÜíArgumentException); deviations None.
- [[compgen-synteny-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001 (synteny / collinearity block detection, MCScanX DP model; Comparative-genomics): reuses [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and supplies its concrete scoring parameters ‚Äî chain DP `Score(v)=max(MatchScore(v), max_u[Score(u)+MatchScore(v)+GapPenalty√óNumberofGaps(u,v)])`, MatchScore 50/GapPenalty ‚àí1/MAX_GAPS 25, report ‚â•250 score (‚â•5 anchor pairs), both transcriptional directions ‚Üí forward + inverted blocks, anchors from BLASTP E‚â§1e-5 (generation delegated to COMPGEN-ORTHO-001); forward(250)/reverse-inverted/4-anchor-200-no-block/25-gap-break/empty oracles; two source-backed assumptions (‚â•250 AND ‚â•5 pairs report rule, orthologMap-supplied anchors); deviations None.
- [[disorder-lc-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-LC-001 (protein low-complexity, SEG / Wootton & Federhen; first of the protein-disorder family): NCBI `blast_seg.c` + GCG/manpage + Wootton-Federhen sources; W=12/K1=2.2/K2=2.5, Shannon-entropy bits/residue two-stage trigger-extend, QQ../AAAAAALLLLLL/AAABBBCCCDDD/12-distinct H=0/1/2/3.585 oracles; X-rich label + greedy-single-residue-extension assumptions; deviations flagged non-boundary-affecting.
- [[disorder-morf-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-MORF-001 (MoRF / Molecular Recognition Feature prediction, dip-in-disorder; second of the protein-disorder family): Mohan 2006 + Cheng/Oldfield PMC2570644 + Oldfield 2005 + Wikipedia sources; ordered dip (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10‚Äì70 flanked both sides by disorder = one MoRF, 0.5 threshold, Œ±/Œ≤/Œπ sub-types, score‚àà[0,1] increases with dip depth; synthetic L-dip-in-P/E-flanks oracle; one assumption = paywalled exact flank-length parameters ‚Üí qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); no contradictions.
- [[disorder-pred-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-PRED-001 (intrinsic-disorder prediction, TOP-IDP sliding window `PredictDisorder`; third of the protein-disorder family): Campen 2008 (TOP-IDP Table 2 + cutoff 0.542 max-likelihood, window 21) + Dunker 2001 (disorder/order/ambiguous sets) + Kyte-Doolittle 1982 + Wikipedia sources; S·µ¢=mean of (p‚àí(‚àí0.884))/1.871 normalized TOP-IDP over window, disordered when ‚â•0.542, all 20 values, W30‚Üí0.0/P30‚Üí1.0/E30‚Üí0.866 oracles, edge-clip + skip-non-canonical (all-unknown‚Üí0.0) + case-insensitive; assumptions None (all params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic (not IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite).
- [[disorder-region-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-REGION-001 (disordered-region detection ‚Äî contiguous-run aggregation + IDR classification over the [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|PredictDisorder]] profile; fifth of the protein-disorder family, enriches the anchor): Campen 2008 + Dunker 2001 + van der Lee 2014 (proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich + short-vs-long‚â•30 subtypes) + Necci 2020 MobiDB-lite 3.0 v3 + Wikipedia sources; contiguous run ‚â• minRegionLength(5) with MeanScore, empty/all-ordered‚Üíno regions / all-disordered‚Üíone region / trailing-region-no-off-by-one oracles; two classification schemes ‚Äî default RegionType (fraction > 0.25 internal ~5√ó-random heuristic) vs opt-in ClassifyRegionFlavorMobiDbLite (charge PA/PPE/NPE/WC via Das&Pappu FCR/NCPR 0.35, composition Cys‚ÜíPro‚ÜíGly‚ÜíSEG‚ÜíPolar at ‚â•0.32, 9-residue window); hand-traced flavor oracles; contradiction flagged = 0.25 is NOT Das&Pappu NCPR (that is a conformational-state threshold); Confidence‚àà[0,1] declared heuristic (MobiDB-lite has none).
- [[disorder-propensity-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 (per-residue disorder propensity ‚Äî raw TOP-IDP lookup + Dunker classification; fourth of the protein-disorder family, reuses the [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] anchor): Campen 2008 (Table 2 raw values, rank-1) + Wikipedia IDP (rank-4, for Dunker sets) + Dunker 2001 (rank-1, citation locator); four primitives `GetDisorderPropensity` (RAW un-normalized value, W‚àí0.884‚Ä¶P+0.987, NOT the [0,1] normalized S·µ¢) / `IsDisorderPromoting` / `DisorderPromotingAminoAcids`={A,E,G,K,P,Q,R,S} / `OrderPromotingAminoAcids`={C,F,I,L,N,V,W,Y}, three sets disjoint+cover-20 (8+8+4); two impl-side assumptions (unknown‚Üí0.0 GetValueOrDefault contract; ranking-string vs Table-2-value S/K discrepancy ‚Üí values authoritative), cutoff 0.542 recorded for completeness but out of this unit's scope; no source contradictions.

- [[meta-func-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit META-FUNC-001 (Functional prediction, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`; fifth Metagenomics family Evidence): Altschul NCBI BLAST-statistics tutorial + NCBI `blast_stat.c` (ungapped BLOSUM62 Œª=0.3176/K=0.134/H=0.4012) + NCBI BLOSUM62 diagonals (W11‚Ä¶) + PNNL ORA ¬ß8.2 sources; homology transfer = exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S ‚Üí bit `S'=(ŒªS‚àílnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=K¬∑m¬∑n¬∑e^(‚àíŒªS)=m¬∑n¬∑2^(‚àíS')`, best hit = lowest E-value (INV-01..03,06); hypergeometric right-tail ORA `P(X‚â•x)=1‚àíŒ£_{i=0}^{x‚àí1}C(M,i)C(N‚àíM,n‚àíi)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, p‚àà[0,1], x=0/M=0/n=0‚Üíp=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWW‚ÜíS33/S'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546e‚àí5 (both forms agree) + ORA N8000/M400/n100/x20‚Üí7.88e‚àí8; one assumption ASM-01 = ungapped exact-match model (affects which hits found, not the formulas); no contradictions. - [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit META-PATHWAY-001 (Pathway enrichment / over-representation analysis, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`; the DEDICATED unit for the ORA machinery that META-FUNC-001 exercises as component B): Boyle et al. 2004 GO::TermFinder (PMC3037731) + PNNL Proteomics ORA ¬ß8.2 (`phyper` reference) sources; hypergeometric right-tail `P(X‚â•x)=1‚àíŒ£_{i=0}^{x‚àí1}C(M,i)C(N‚àíM,n‚àíi)/C(N,n)` (N=background/M=pathway size/n=query/x=overlap), `phyper(x‚àí1,M,N‚àíM,n,lower.tail=FALSE)`, log-Gamma summation, p‚àà[0,1], sorted ascending; x=0/M=0/n=0‚Üíp=1 corner cases, M‚Üîn symmetry; oracles PNNL N8000/M100/n400/x20‚Üí7.88e‚àí8 + exact rational 1/252 (all overlap) / 5/6 (partial) / 1 (no overlap) / 251/252 (at-least-one); one assumption = background defaults to union-of-pathway-members when caller supplies none (formula-preserving, caller-overridable); no FDR correction; no contradictions. - [[onco-sv-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-SV-001 (somatic complex-rearrangement classification / chromothripsis inference; thirty-fourth Oncology unit, first complex-SV method): Korbel & Campbell 2013 Cell (six hallmark criteria A‚ÄìF; criterion A clustering = exponential-null inter-breakpoint distances; criterion B oscillating between canonically **two** CN states; clustering necessary-but-not-sufficient) + Maher & Wilson review PMC3861665 (Magrangeas 2011 first-pass **‚â•10 oscillating-CN-change** screen; two-state hallmark; exponential null) + Cort√©s-Ciriano 2020 Nat Genet (PCAWG 2,658 genomes ‚Äî high-confidence **‚â•7** adjacent oscillating segments / low **4‚Äì6** / <4 not-called; canonical **>60%** two-state fraction; minimum **6** clustered intrachromosomal SVs) + Magrangeas 2011 Blood sources; worked oracles `2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2`‚Üí10 oscillations two-state‚ÜíChromothripsis, `2,1,2,1,2,1`‚Üí5<10‚ÜíNotComplex, `2,3,4,5,6,7` monotone‚Üí0 oscillations/>2 states‚ÜíNotComplex (progressive amplification/BFB); two operationalisation assumptions (oscillation = adjacent-segment CN-state-reversal count with ‚â§3-state bound; breakpoint clustering = CV>1 vs exponential CV=1); no contradictions. Own concept [[chromothripsis-inference]] (consumes the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]).
- [[onco-tmb-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-TMB-001 (Tumor Mutational Burden ‚Äî mutations/Mb + TMB-high classification; thirty-fifth Oncology unit): Chalmers 2017 Genome Medicine 9:34 PMC5395719 (rank 1, TMB = "number of somatic, coding, base substitution, and indel mutations per megabase"; FoundationOne 315-gene = 1.1 Mb; synonymous counted to reduce noise; COSMIC/tumor-suppressor/dbSNP/ExAC germline/driver removed before counting; <0.5 Mb panel-vs-WES deviation rises) + Marcus 2021 FDA Approval Summary Clin Cancer Res 27(17):4685 PMC8416776 (rank 2, TMB-High ‚â° TMB ‚â• 10 mut/Mb inclusive, pembrolizumab tumor-agnostic approval June 16 2020, F1CDx companion diagnostic) + Merino 2020 Friends of Cancer Research TMB Harmonization Project PMC7710563 (rank 1‚Äì2, mut/Mb reporting unit + ‚â•10 cutoff confirmation, F1CDx ~0.8 Mb/324 genes) sources; oracles 11/1.1‚Üí10.0 High ¬∑ 300/30‚Üí10.0 High ¬∑ 150/10‚Üí15.0 High ¬∑ 99/10‚Üí9.9 not-High ¬∑ 100/10‚Üí10.0 High(boundary) ¬∑ 0‚Üínot-High; corner cases targetRegionMb=0‚Üídiv-by-zero throws ¬∑ negative count/region rejected ¬∑ <0.5 Mb computes but known-unstable ¬∑ TMB monotone in count/region; one flagged conflict (unsupported registry three-tier Low<6/Intermediate 6‚Äì20/High>20 ‚Äî no source for 6/20 boundaries ‚Äî resolved to the single source-backed two-tier ‚â•10 cutoff); no contradictions. Own concept [[tumor-mutational-burden]] (counts the caller-supplied somatic list of [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]], sibling immunotherapy biomarker of [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]).
- [[onco-vaf-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-VAF-001 (Variant Allele Frequency Analysis ‚Äî empirical VAF + Wilson binomial CI + purity/ploidy correction; thirty-sixth Oncology unit): GATK Mutect2 FAQ (rank 3, empirical VAF = altReads/totalReads = alt AD / sum AD, distinct from the model-estimate `AF` FORMAT field) + Wikipedia Binomial-proportion-CI / Wilson 1927 JASA 22(158):209‚Äì212 (rank 4/1, Wilson score interval `center=(pÃÇ+z¬≤/2n)/(1+z¬≤/n)` / `margin=(z/(1+z¬≤/n))¬∑‚àö(pÃÇ(1‚àípÃÇ)/n+z¬≤/4n¬≤)`, z=1.96 for 95%, no-overshoot/non-zero-width vs criticised Wald) + Tarabichi 2017/2021 PMC5538405 (rank 1, diploid het clonal expected VAF = purity√ó0.5) + CNAqc Househam/Caravagna *Genome Biology* 2024 25:38 (rank 1, expected VAF `v=mœÄ/(2(1‚àíœÄ)+œÄ¬∑n_tot)`, 33%/66% 2:1 peaks, inversion `m¬∑CCF = VAF¬∑(2(1‚àíœÄ)+œÄ¬∑n_tot)/œÄ` = `AdjustVAFForPurity`) sources; oracles empirical 25/100‚Üí0.25 ¬∑ 0/10‚Üí0.00 ¬∑ 10/10‚Üí1.00, Wilson (25,100)‚Üí0.2592 [0.1755,0.3430] & (0,10)‚Üí[0.0000,0.2775] / (10,10)‚Üí[0.7225,1.0000], correction (0.40,0.80,2)‚Üí1.00 / (0.20,0.50,2)‚Üí0.80 / (0.30,0.50,4)‚Üí1.80; corner cases VAF>1 alignment-artifact‚Üíinvalid, totalReads=0‚Üí0/0 guarded, purity œÄ=0‚Üíundefined; two source-backed assumptions (z=1.96 verbatim not 1.959964, `AdjustVAFForPurity` normal CN=2 diploid background); no contradictions. Own concept [[variant-allele-frequency-and-binomial-ci]] (the foundational VAF primitive; empirical VAF shared with [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] / [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]], CNAqc inversion shared with [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]).
- [[pangen-cluster-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PANGEN-CLUSTER-001 (Gene Clustering ‚Äî greedy incremental homolog grouping by sequence identity; first pan-genome PANGEN-* unit): Li & Godzik 2006 (CD-HIT) + CD-HIT User's Guide (`-c`/`-G 1` global-identity, greedy long‚Üíshort incremental) + Page et al. 2015 (Roary pan-genome context, default 95% ortholog identity) + EMBOSS needle (identical-aligned-positions numerator) sources; global identity = identical positions / alignment length, greedy first-match representative assignment; no source contradictions; two assumptions (alignment-free/no-internal-indel identity may underestimate; homolog groups only, no synteny/paralog-split step). - [[pangen-core-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PANGEN-CORE-001 (Core/accessory/unique pan-genome partition + genomic fluidity + open/closed; second PANGEN-* unit): Tettelin 2005 (pan-genome/core/accessory) + Tettelin 2008 (open ‚ü∫ alpha<1) + Kislyuk 2011 (fluidity formula + jackknife variance) + Page et al. 2015 (Roary fractional 99% core, hard-core/soft-core/shell/cloud) + micropan (`heaps()` alpha, `fluidity()`) + Wikipedia sources; `ConstructPanGenome` occupancy partition with fractional rule `occupancy/N ‚â• coreFraction` (**not** `floor(coreFraction¬∑N)`), fluidity `œÜ=[2/(N(N‚àí1))]¬∑Œ£(U_k+U_l)/(M_k+M_l)` ‚àà[0,1] (3-genome oracle 10/18=0.5ÃÑ, bounds 0/1), open/closed by Heaps alpha; corner cases <3 genomes degenerate openness, N<2 fluidity 0, empty-pair term 0; two assumptions (clustering delegated to `ClusterGenes` k-mer Jaccard, empty-pair‚Üí0); no contradictions. Own concept [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]].
- [[pangen-marker-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PANGEN-MARKER-001 (Phylogenetic Marker Selection ‚Äî single-copy core genes ranked by parsimony-informative sites; fourth PANGEN-* unit): Ding/Baumdicker/Neher 2018 (panX ‚Äî single-copy core "all strains represented exactly once", extracts variable positions ‚Üí FastTree, recombination caveat) + Page et al. 2015 (Roary 99% core, paralog split into true orthologs) + Roary docs (paralog clusters filtered from core gene alignment) + Zvelebil & Baum 2008 (parsimony-informative site = ‚â•2 states, each in ‚â•2 sequences) sources; `SelectPhylogeneticMarkers` keeps single-copy core clusters with PIS‚â•1 ranked by descending PIS capped at `maxMarkers`, `CountParsimonyInformativeSites` scores columns; oracles `AAAAA`/`AAACA`/`AACCG`/`ACCTG`‚ÜíPIS 2 (cols 3,5; mono/singleton/4-singleton excluded), 3-genome selection excludes paralog/not-core/0-PIS-conserved; one assumption (no in-repo aligner ‚Üí PIS over equal-length members position-wise, unequal‚ÜíPIS 0); no contradictions. - [[pangen-heap-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PANGEN-HEAP-001 (Pan-Genome Growth Model ‚Äî Heaps'-law fit of the new-gene curve; third PANGEN-* unit): micropan `heaps()` (rank 3, model `y=K¬∑x^(-alpha)`, count>0‚Üí1 binarization, first-appearance new-gene rule `(cm==1)[i]&(cm==0)[i-1]`, genome index starts at 2, n.perm=100, objective `J=sqrt(Œ£(y‚àíK¬∑x^(-alpha))¬≤)/|x|` over K‚àà[0,10000]/alpha‚àà[0,2], verbatim "alpha<1 open, alpha>1 closed") + Tettelin 2008 (power-law openness) + Tettelin 2005 (*S. agalactiae* anchor: 161/54 new genes, tg(Œ∏)=33, ‚âà80% core, open) sources; exact oracles x=[2,3] y=[8,4]‚Üíalpha ln2/ln(3/2)‚âà1.7095 K‚âà26.164 closed, constant y=[1,1]‚Üíalpha 0 K 1 open; corner cases <2 genomes degenerate (no exception), binary presence only, alpha=1 boundary not-open; two assumptions (optimizer method non-correctness-affecting, fixed-seed permutation RNG); no contradictions. - [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-BOOT-001 (Phylogenetic Bootstrap Analysis ‚Äî Felsenstein's bootstrap proportions; first phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Felsenstein 1985 *Evolution* 39(4):783 (origin ‚Äî resample characters with replacement, same sample size, keep species; *P* = fraction of bootstrap samples a group appears in; 95%‚Üísignificant) + Lemoine 2018 *Nature* 556:452 PMC6030568 (same-length pseudo-alignments; support = proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch; branch = bipartition; binary per-replicate) + Biopython `Bio.Phylo.Consensus` (`bootstrap`/`bootstrap_trees`/`get_support` ‚Äî column resample `randint(0,length-1)`, clades matched **by terminal leaf-name set**, only `find_clades(terminal=False)` scored, `(t+1)*100/size`) sources; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor 100 reps seed 42 ‚Üí support{A,B}=support{C,D}=1.0 (saturated JC distances ‚Üí identical topology every replicate), all-identical `ACGTACGT`‚Üíevery clade 1.0; MUST-test support‚àà[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / support=k/replicates, input validation null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage √ó100); no contradictions. Own concept [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]].
- [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-COMP-001 (Tree Comparison ‚Äî Robinson‚ÄìFoulds distance, MRCA, patristic distance; second phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Robinson‚ÄìFoulds metric / MRCA / Phylogenetic tree + Robinson & Foulds 1981 (doi:10.1016/0025-5564(81)90043-2, RF proper metric via splits) + Smith 2020 (generalized RF) + Day 1985 (linear-time) sources; RF = symmetric difference `A+B` of canonical split sets (raw count, even, rooted-clade = dummy-leaf), **max RF = 2(n‚àí2) rooted vs 2(n‚àí3) unrooted** reconciled by dummy-leaf equivalence; MRCA O(n) recursive leaf-name traversal (not-in-tree‚Üínull), patristic = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` (not-in-tree‚ÜíNaN, zero-branches‚Üí0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/‚â•0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/‚â•0; two source-backed scope decisions (binary-only via `PhyloNode` Left/Right, rooted-only via UPGMA/NJ); no deviations, no contradictions. Own concept [[tree-comparison-metrics]].
- [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-DIST-001 (Phylogenetic Distance Matrix Calculation; third phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Models-of-DNA-evolution / Substitution-model / Distance-matrices-in-phylogeny + Jukes & Cantor 1969 + Kimura 1980 + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`) / **JC69** (`-3/4¬∑ln(1‚àí4p/3)`) / **K2P** (`-1/2¬∑ln((1‚àí2S‚àíV)¬∑‚àö(1‚àí2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *n√ón*, correction ordering JC69‚â•p & K2P‚â•p, triangle-inequality expected-not-guaranteed; pairwise deletion (gaps + IUPAC N/R/Y skipped), case-insensitive; **JC69 saturates p‚â•3/4‚Üí+‚àû / K2P V‚â•1/2‚Üí+‚àû**, all-gap/empty‚Üí0, unequal-length‚ÜíArgumentException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`‚ÜíHamming 1/p 0.125/JC69‚âà0.137, transition `GCGT` K2P‚âà0.34657 vs transversion `CCGT`‚âà0.31713, mixed‚âà0.30679, gap‚Üí7 sites; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gap‚Üí0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions. Own concept [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]].
- [[phylo-newick-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-NEWICK-001 (Newick I/O ‚Äî `ToNewick`/`ParseNewick`, the phylogenetics serialization layer): Wikipedia Newick format + PHYLIP (Felsenstein) + Olsen 1990 "8:45 Tree Format" BNF sources; nested-paren grammar `Tree‚ÜíSubtree ";"`, leaf names, `:`-branch lengths, internal labels, Olsen root `[label][:len]`, multifurcation/unnamed/single-taxon admitted; label rules (no `()[]':;,`), invariants N1‚ÄìN9 (`;`-terminate, leaf-count match, round-trip preserves topology+names, InvariantCulture `.` decimals, empty‚Üíthrow, null‚Üíempty, scientific notation, balanced-paren recursive descent); scope limits binary-only / no quoted labels / no `[]` comments / no underscore‚Üíblank / F4 ¬±0.00005; no deviations, no contradictions. Serializer, not a new algorithm ‚Äî no own concept; cross-links [[tree-comparison-metrics]] / [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] / [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]].
- [[phylo-stats-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-STATS-001 (Tree Statistics ‚Äî leaves, total tree length, tree depth/height; phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Tree-(graph-theory)/Tree-(abstract-data-type) (leaf=no-children; **depth**=root-path length, root 0; **height**=longest downward path to a leaf in **edges**, tree height=root height; single-node 0; **empty tree ‚àí1**) + Biopython `Bio.Phylo.BaseTree` (`get_terminals`/`count_terminals`/`is_terminal`/`total_branch_length`=Œ£ branch lengths) + DendroPy `Tree.length()` (Œ£ edge lengths, **missing length‚Üí0**) + Wikipedia Minimum-evolution (total branch length as the ME quantity, Rzhetsky & Nei 1992) sources; `GetLeaves` (terminal nodes) / `CalculateTreeLength` (Œ£ all branch lengths) / `GetTreeDepth` (height in edges); worked oracles balanced `((A:1,B:1):1,(C:1,D:1):1)`‚Üí4 leaves/length 6/height 2, caterpillar `(A:1,(B:1,(C:1,D:1)))` (internal 0.5)‚Üí4/5/3, single leaf‚Üí1/branch-len/0, null root‚Üí‚àÖ/0/‚àí1; one assumption (null `PhyloNode`‚Üîempty-tree convention: `GetTreeDepth(null)`‚Üí‚àí1, leaves/length‚Üí‚àÖ/0); no deviations, no contradictions. Own concept [[tree-statistics]].
- [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-TREE-001 (Phylogenetic Tree Construction ‚Äî UPGMA & Neighbor-Joining; the phylogenetics PHYLO-* tree-building core): Wikipedia UPGMA / Neighbor-joining / Phylogenetic-tree + Saitou & Nei 1987 (MBE 4(4):406‚Äì425, NJ) + Sokal & Michener 1958 (UPGMA) + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `BuildTree`/`BuildTreeFromMatrix` consume the distance matrix and emit a `PhyloNode` tree via two agglomerative methods ‚Äî **UPGMA** (rooted ultrametric, molecular clock, **height=d/2**, arithmetic-mean update, O(n¬≥)/O(n¬≤)) and **NJ** (unrooted/midpoint-rooted, clock-free, **Q(i,j)=(n‚àí2)¬∑d(i,j)‚àíŒ£d(i,k)‚àíŒ£d(j,k)** join minimum-Q, Œ¥(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(Œ£d(f,k)‚àíŒ£d(g,k))/(2(n‚àí2)), additive-matrix topology guarantee, **negative branches preserved, not clamped**, O(n¬≥)); invariants all-taxa-leaves / binary / n leaves+n‚àí1 internal / UPGMA branches‚â•0 / UPGMA ultrametric+rooted / NJ additive-correct+may-be-negative+no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA matrix‚Üí(a,b)@17‚Üí((a,b),e)@22‚Üí(c,d)@28‚Üífinal@33, Œ¥(a,u)=8.5/Œ¥(e,v)=11/Œ¥(c,w)=14/root 16.5 (tips all 16.5, tol 1e-10), NJ 5-taxon‚Üífirst join (a,b) **Q‚ÇÅ(a,b)=‚àí50**, Œ¥(a,u)=2/Œ¥(b,u)=3/Œ¥(u,v)=3/Œ¥(c,v)=4/Œ¥(v,w)=2/Œ¥(d,w)=2/Œ¥(e,w)=1 (patristic recovers input); edge cases <2/unequal‚Üíthrow, identical‚Üíarbitrary join, all-equal‚Üístar, saturated p>0.75‚ÜíJC +‚àû; 32 runs (M01‚ÄìM13/S01‚ÄìS05/C01‚ÄìC05), S06 removed (dup of S02); deviations None (¬ß8). Own concept [[distance-based-tree-construction]].

## Concepts

- [[three-front-doors]] ‚Äî one algorithm engine exposed through skills, the C# API, and MCP, with identical results.
- [[skill-layer]] ‚Äî the Agent-Skill routing + discipline layer that keeps 427 tool schemas out of the model's context.
- [[layered-architecture]] ‚Äî the strict up-only dependency layering (Levels 0‚Äì4) enforced by architecture tests.
- [[scientific-rigor]] ‚Äî runtime honesty: `LimitationPolicy`, tool-only computation, provenance on every result.
- [[validation-and-testing]] ‚Äî 22k+ tests across ten methodologies plus the per-unit validation campaign.
- [[property-based-testing]] ‚Äî P0 methodology (FsCheck): hundreds of generated inputs checked against expressible invariants (R/S/I/M/P/RT/D); 258/258.
- [[metamorphic-testing]] ‚Äî P0 methodology: metamorphic relations across runs (SUB/MON/INV/SYM/COMP/SHIFT) that solve the oracle problem; 258/258, ~200+ relations.
- [[fuzzing]] ‚Äî P2 methodology: random/malformed/boundary input for clean-failure; parsers the hot target; zero‚Üí258/258.
- [[snapshot-testing]] ‚Äî P1 methodology (Verify): golden-master `.verified.txt` regression capture; the least-complete methodology at 37/255.
- [[algebraic-testing]] ‚Äî P1 methodology: explicit algebraic laws (identity/associativity/involution/round-trip‚Ä¶); 89 applicable + 169 not-applicable.
- [[architecture-testing]] ‚Äî P2 methodology (ArchUnitNET): 22 IL-level module rules enforcing the [[layered-architecture]] Dependency Rule; scales by module not algorithm.
- [[differential-testing]] ‚Äî P2 methodology: two independent implementations cross-checked (ALT/BRUTE/REF/DUAL); 107/255.
- [[combinatorial-testing]] ‚Äî P3 methodology: minimal pairwise parameter-interaction coverage; 193/255 + 65 not-applicable.
- [[characterization-testing]] ‚Äî P3 methodology: golden-master pinning of behaviour before refactors (invariance, not correctness); on-demand.
- [[build-quality-gate]] ‚Äî the build-time static-analysis gate: SonarAnalyzer ratcheted to blocking under `TreatWarningsAsErrors`, fix-or-silence, review-not-blind-fix.
- [[test-unit-registry]] ‚Äî the area-prefixed Test Unit ID scheme and per-unit record behind the validation effort.
- [[definition-of-done]] ‚Äî the six-criterion acceptance bar (TestSpec, tests, ‚â•80% coverage, edge cases, CI, evidence) each unit must clear.
- [[algorithm-validation-evidence]] ‚Äî the templated per-unit `docs/Evidence/` artifact pattern (sources, worked-example dataset, deviations) behind the "Evidence documented" DoD criterion.
- [[global-alignment-needleman-wunsch]] ‚Äî the canonical DP global-alignment algorithm (`GlobalAlign`): linear-gap recurrence, O(nm), traceback, affine-as-extension.
- [[multiple-sequence-alignment]] ‚Äî aligning 3+ sequences (NP-complete): Seqeron's star (`MultipleAlign`), iterative-refinement (MUSCLE), and consistency (T-Coffee) aligners; sum-of-pairs + consensus.
- [[semi-global-alignment-fitting]] ‚Äî ends-free "glocal" alignment: fitting/query-in-reference variant (Rosalind SIMS); NW recurrence with free reference end gaps, traceback from max of last row.
- [[alignment-statistics]] ‚Äî post-alignment metrics: percent identity/similarity/gaps (EMBOSS/BLAST convention, denominator includes gaps, positive-score ‚áí similar) and srspair three-line markup.
- [[coding-potential-hexamer-score]] ‚Äî CPAT hexamer usage-bias coding-potential score: mean of ln(coding/noncoding) over in-frame hexamers (wordSize 6/step 3), sign convention, ¬±1 pseudo-scores; Fickett TESTCODE as not-implemented alternative.
- [[relative-synonymous-codon-usage]] ‚Äî RSCU (Sharp & Li 1986) codon-usage-bias measure: n_i¬∑x/Œ£x normalization, 1.0=no bias, bounded [0,n_i], Œ£-over-family=n_i invariant; pooled counts, sense codons only; base anchor of the codon-usage family (vs CAI's max-normalization).
- [[codon-adaptation-index]] ‚Äî CAI (Sharp & Li 1987) whole-gene codon-bias / expression-proxy score in [0,1]: geometric mean of relative adaptiveness w=f/max_synonym_f, low-value-sensitive, stop excluded; dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode (exclude can give L=0‚Üí0); E. coli oracles; Seqeron deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (vs Sharp & Li's 0.5 reference-table pseudocount); one level above RSCU.
- [[rare-codon-analysis]] ‚Äî codon-usage family's *localization/diagnostic* unit (`FindRareCodons` + cluster addendum): a codon is rare when its per-family frequency < threshold (default 0.15), reports position/AA/frequency (E. coli AGA 0.04/AGG 0.02/CGA 0.06/CUA 0.04); addendum adds two published cluster methods ‚Äî Clarke & Clark 2008 %MinMax (18-codon window, signed %Min/%Max ‚àà[‚àí100,+100], rare clusters = negative peaks) and Chartier 2012 Sherlocc (7-codon window, ‚â•4 of 7 freq‚â§threshold "slow" positions = a rare-codon cluster); single-codon-AA contributes 0 to %MinMax (no NaN), overlapping windows merged; feeds [[codon-optimization]]'s AvoidRareCodons; oracles ‚àí86.36/+100/+36.47% and 7√óAGA‚Üí1 cluster; deviations None.
- [[codon-usage-comparison]] ‚Äî codon-usage family's *raw* end (`CalculateCodonUsage` + `CompareCodonUsage`): unnormalized codon-count table (non-overlapping triplets, T‚ÜíU, drop partial codon, Dictionary<codon,int>, Œ£counts=total invariant) + Total Variation Distance similarity `1‚àíŒ£|f‚ÇÅ‚àíf‚ÇÇ|/2 ‚àà [0,1]` between two codon-frequency distributions; proven identity 1.0 / symmetry / range [0,1] / disjoint‚Üí0 / partial-overlap-exact properties; empty‚Üí0, TVD-not-cosine deliberate metric choice; Kazusa-verified organism tables; shares RSCU's counting primitive, the distribution-comparison op none of the bias measures provide.
- [[codon-optimization]] ‚Äî codon-usage family's CDS-*rewriting* operation (`OptimizeSequence`): synonymous substitution to improve host expression; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression=Mignon 2018 / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondary‚ÜíReduceSecondaryStructure); invariants protein-preservation + Met/AUG & Trp/UGG fixed + stop preserved + CAI‚àà(0,1]; RNA notation, T‚ÜíU, trim-to-codon, 1e-6 CAI clamp; E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon fixtures; actuator to RSCU/CAI/ENC's measurement.
- [[effective-number-of-codons]] ‚Äî ENC/Nc (Wright 1990) reference-free whole-gene codon-bias measure in [20,61]: reciprocal of codon homozygosity FÃÇ=(n¬∑Œ£p¬≤‚àí1)/(n‚àí1) aggregated by degeneracy class (Nc=2+9/FÃÇ‚ÇÇ+1/FÃÇ‚ÇÉ+5/FÃÇ‚ÇÑ+3/FÃÇ‚ÇÜ); 20=max bias / 61=uniform, unbiased‚Üí61, no-bias-sim‚Üí40.5; Ile absent‚Üí(FÃÇ‚ÇÇ+FÃÇ‚ÇÑ)/2 fallback, overshoot re-adjusts to 61; reference-free counterpart of CAI; one assumption = non-source-prescribed lower clamp at 20.
- [[repetitive-element-detection]] ‚Äî repeats/tandem family anchor: tandem (head-to-tail, ‚â•2 copies, primitive unit), inverted (W¬∑G¬∑WÃÑ·¥ø / zero-gap palindrome, IUPACpal), and RepeatMasker-class assignment; ClassifyRepeat = exact-substring containment, not Smith-Waterman homology.
- [[consensus-sequence]] ‚Äî assembly CONSENSUS family anchor: column-wise majority/threshold consensus (Biopython dumb_consensus rule) ‚Äî gaps skipped, emit iff unique max and freq ‚â• threshold else ambiguous, tie‚Üíambiguous, all-gap‚ÜíN no div-by-zero; N/0.5 parameterized defaults; shared with MSA consensus step.
- [[consensus-from-alignment]] ‚Äî Motif-Analysis consensus-from-a-multiple-alignment (MOTIF-CONS-001, `MotifFinder.CreateConsensusFromAlignment`): pure most-frequent (plurality) column consensus over equal-length aligned strings, deterministic alphabetical tie-break (A<C<G<T), no threshold (always emits); Rosalind CONS `ATGCAACT` oracle; `alternative_to` the threshold/tie‚Üíambiguous assembly [[consensus-sequence]], motif-family sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] ‚Äî MotifFinder degenerate-consensus unit (MOTIF-GENERATE-001, `MotifFinder.GenerateConsensus`): collapses equal-length aligned columns into an IUPAC-ambiguity-coded string ‚Äî per column keep every base with `count > 0.25¬∑n` (strict `>`), emit the NC-IUB 1984 symbol for that base set (R/Y/S/W/K/M, B/D/H/V, N), no-pass fallback ‚Üí most-frequent (alphabetical tie); DECIPHER threshold-consensus family + NC-IUB/UCSC/Wikipedia bijective set‚Üísymbol table; `A,A,G,G,C`‚ÜíR / strict-`>` boundary / four-way‚ÜíA-fallback oracles; `alternative_to` the plurality [[consensus-from-alignment]], degenerate sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[regulatory-element-detection]] ‚Äî Motif-Discovery regulatory-element unit (MOTIF-REGULATORY-001, `KnownMotifs` catalog scan): matches a **fixed, cited catalog of 12 canonical regulatory consensus elements** (TATA/‚àí10/‚àí35/CAAT/GC promoter boxes, Kozak + Shine-Dalgarno translation signals, poly(A), and E-box/AP-1/NF-Œ∫B/CREB TF sites) against a DNA sequence, reporting each occurrence's Name/Pattern/Sequence at its 0-based start; mixes exact and one IUPAC-degenerate (E-box `CANNTG`) match; anchors the AP-1 corrected-consensus regression (`TGAGTCA`‚Üí`TGACTCA`, `AATGAGTCAGG`‚Üí0 hits); two source-backed representative-site assumptions (NF-Œ∫B `GGGACTTTCC`, Kozak `GCCGCCACCATGG`); the curated-biological-catalog specialization of the generic exact [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the generation-direction [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] ‚Äî Motif-Discovery de-novo unit (MOTIF-DISCOVER-001, `MotifFinder.DiscoverMotifs`): finds **unknown** over-represented motifs by enumerating every length-`k` k-mer, counting overlapping occurrences, and ranking by observed/expected enrichment `Count/((N‚àík+1)/4^k)` under a zero-order i.i.d. uniform background (Compeau & Pevzner); deterministic exact single-pass, 0-based positions; `ATGC` in `ATGCATGCATGC` k=4 ‚Üí 768/9‚âà85.333, `AAA` in `AAAAAAAAAA` k=3 ‚Üí 64.0 oracles; `k>N`‚Üíempty, minCount presentation-only, zero-order-only + no-p-value simplifications; the de-novo inverse of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and distinct from the [[consensus-from-alignment]] plurality consensus.
- [[shared-motifs]] ‚Äî Motif-Discovery cross-sequence unit (MOTIF-SHARED-001, `FindSharedMotifs`): the van Helden / RSAT oligo-analysis **"matching sequences"** quorum ‚Äî enumerate every fixed-`k` exact word across a *set* of sequences and report each word present in ‚â• `minSequences` of them (each carrying its `SequenceIndices` set + `Prevalence`=matching/total); a within-sequence repeat counts **1** (presence/absence, not multiplicity); exact-word only (no degenerate/substitution); the cross-sequence sibling of the single-sequence O/E [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] and `alternative_to` the fixed-k-quorum-vs-single-longest LCSM framing of [[longest-common-substring]] (returns all qualifying words, not one longest present in all).
- [[approximate-pattern-matching-mismatches]] ‚Äî pattern-matching PAT-APPROX family anchor (PAT-APPROX-003): Hamming-distance **approximate matching** ‚Äî a `k`-mer appears with ‚â§`d` mismatches when `HammingDistance(P,P')‚â§d` (BA1H); `Count_d`/`FindApproximateOccurrences` scan windows, `FindFrequentKmersWithMismatches` (BA1I) ranks `k`-mers by their **d-neighborhood** (Hamming-ball) tally so the winner need not occur exactly, `Neighbors` (BA1N) enumerates the ball (includes identity), `FindBestMatch` returns the leftmost min-Hamming window; oracles {GATG,ATGC,ATGT} count 5, {6,7,26,27,78}, Count_1=4, ACG/1‚Üí10; d=0 degenerates to exact so it is the mismatch-tolerant `alternative_to` [[k-mer-positions]] and the fuzzy sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] / de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; substitution-only (no indels ‚Äî that is the alignment family), deviations none.
- [[coverage-depth-calculation]] ‚Äî assembly COVER family anchor: per-base sequencing depth over a reference (count of placed reads spanning each position, exact); average depth = Œ£depth/G = Lander-Waterman C=LN/G, breadth = covered/G = 1‚àíe^‚àíc; boundary-clip + empty-input rules; ACGTTGCAAT‚Üí1.5/1.0 oracle; Poisson (e^‚àíc gap) as a property check only; read placement (minOverlap best-match) out of scope.
- [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]] ‚Äî assembly DBG family anchor: k-mer graph (distinct (k-1)-mers = nodes, each k-mer = one prefix‚Üísuffix edge, directed multigraph) + Eulerian-walk reconstruction (balanced/semi-balanced, Euler theorems 8.1/8.2, O(|E|) Hierholzer); spelling = path[0]+last char of each node; unique-walk oracles only (AAABBBA, a_long‚Ä¶, to_every‚Ä¶ k=4, ATGGCGTGCA); repeat/gap/error ‚Üí non-Eulerian; walk-selection unspecified so exact asserts on unique-walk inputs; OLC is the alternative formulation.
- [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]] ‚Äî assembly OLC family anchor: the three-stage Overlap-Layout-Consensus paradigm (`FindAllOverlaps` + `AssembleOLC`) ‚Äî overlap graph (read=node, edge on longest suffix-of-A/prefix-of-B ‚â• threshold), Layout = Hamiltonian path (NP-complete) + transitive reduction + non-branching contigs, Consensus = majority vote; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling oracles; suffix-tree O(N+a) vs all-pairs O(N¬≤); NP-complete/repeat-split/greedy-suboptimal failure modes; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions; Hamiltonian/overlap-graph alternative to DBG's Eulerian/k-mer formulation.
- [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]] ‚Äî assembly MERGE family anchor: suffix‚Äìprefix overlap collapse primitive (`MergeContigs`) behind greedy SCS and OLC layout; overlap = length-l suffix of X = prefix of Y, longest match reported, collapse keeps one copy so |merge|=|c1|+|c2|‚àíl; overlap 0 / out-of-range ‚Üí plain concatenation; BAA+AAB‚ÜíBAAB, chain‚ÜíAAABBBA oracles; caller-trusts-length + out-of-range‚Üíconcat API-contract assumptions; overlap-based sibling of DBG's k-mer/Eulerian formulation.
- [[scaffolding]] ‚Äî assembly SCAFFOLD family anchor: joining ordered contigs into a scaffold, adjacent contigs separated by `N`-runs of length = the (upstream) inter-contig distance estimate (ABySS 2.0 rule); positive gap `g` ‚Üí `g`√ó`N`, scaffold length = Œ£|contig|+Œ£gap; non-positive (zero/negative) estimate ‚Üí AGP unknown-size default 100 N (negative = overlap, unresolved here); each contig in ‚â§1 scaffold, unlinked ‚Üí singleton; parameterized fill char; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; downstream of DBG/OLC/merge, hands off to contig-merge on the negative-gap overlap case; 100-constant source-backed (INSDC), only the fall-back-not-resolve decision is assumed.
- [[assembly-statistics]] ‚Äî assembly STATS family anchor: contiguity/QC summary metrics over contig lengths (read-only, downstream of DBG/OLC/merge/scaffold) ‚Äî Nx = shortest length covering ‚â•x% (largest-first, inclusive ‚â•; N50/N90), Lx = the matching contig count, N90 ‚â§ N50 / L90 ‚â• L50, auN = Œ£L·µ¢¬≤/Œ£L‚±º (area under Nx curve, more stable than N50); + totals/largest/smallest/GC and 0-based inclusive N-run gaps; Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST + Heng Li 2020; Assembly A N50 70/L50 2, auN 73.333 oracles; empty‚Üízeros (not None) + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[quality-trimming-running-sum]] ‚Äî assembly TRIM family anchor: BWA/cutadapt running-sum quality trimming ‚Äî subtract cutoff from each Phred quality, take partial sums to the 3' end, cut at the minimum (= BWA argmax of accumulated threshold‚àíq, with `s<0` early break + `BWA_MIN_RDLEN=35` floor); Phred+33 decode (Cock 2010); `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10‚Üífirst 4 bases oracle; threshold<1 disables / all-high unchanged / all-low dropped / good-base-among-bad refinement; both-end pass + downstream minLength filter as assumptions; read-QC preprocessing upstream of correction/DBG/OLC.
- [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]] ‚Äî assembly CORRECT family anchor: two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction (Musket/Quake) ‚Äî trusted (multiplicity > cut-off) vs untrusted k-mers, base trusted if covered by any trusted k-mer, unique alternative making all covering k-mers trusted, ambiguity/no-set‚Üíunchanged; substitution-only (count+length preserved); kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 non-behavioral defaults.
- [[centromere-analysis]] ‚Äî chromosome centromere/alpha-satellite family anchor (second Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeCentromere` + 4 additive detectors ‚Äî Levan 1964 q/p arm-ratio classes (Metacentric ‚â§1.7 / Submetacentric ‚â§3.0 / Subtelocentric <7.0 / Acrocentric ‚â•7.0 / Telocentric p=0); alpha-satellite-specific `DetectAlphaSatellite`/`FindCenpBBoxes` (171-bp tandem period ¬±5, AT>0.5, 17-bp CENP-B box `YTTCGTTGGAARCGGGA`, no embedded monomer); `DetectHigherOrderRepeat` (HOR period = smallest k with monomers k apart ‚â•95% identical across ‚â•90%, intra-HOR 50‚Äì70% vs inter-HOR 97‚Äì100%); `AssignSuprachromosomalFamily` (bundled CC0 Dfam ALR/ALRa=A/ALRb=B, SF3 pentameric/SF4 monomeric/{SF1,SF2} dimeric/SF5 irregular); base AlphaSatelliteContent is density-heuristic-not-specific + SF1/SF2-unresolved (non-redistributable consensus library) limitations.
- [[karyotype-analysis]] ‚Äî chromosome karyotyping/ploidy-detection family anchor (third Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeKaryotype` builds a karyotype from chromosome descriptors (split sex/autosome, group by base name, count copies, compare to expected ploidy, label nullisomy..pentasomy by absolute count; TotalChromosomes/TotalGenomeSize/MeanChromosomeLength invariants) and `DetectPloidy` estimates whole-genome ploidy from read depth (true-median ratio ‚Üí round(ratio√ó2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1‚àí|ratio√ó2‚àíploidy|√ó2, empty‚Üí(2,0)); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD4 nullisomy-unreachable-via-GroupBy, DD5 disomy-only-aneuploid-in-polyploid; deviations None. Descriptor-count sibling of depth-log-ratio [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] ‚Äî shared synteny anchor (fourth Chromosome-analysis unit; comparative-genomics COMPGEN-SYNTENY will reuse it): `FindSyntenyBlocks` builds syntenic blocks from ortholog pairs (group by chr pair, sort by ref position, collinear runs merged under maxGap, emit ‚â•minGenes; block carries strand '+'/'-', GeneCount, SequenceIdentity=NaN for coordinate-only input per MCScanX; I1‚ÄìI5) + `DetectRearrangements` classifies adjacent-block signals (diff target chr‚ÜíTranslocation, same chr diff strand‚ÜíInversion, gap asymmetry‚ÜíDeletion, overlapping source diff targets‚ÜíDuplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation(50000)/inversion(size 10000) oracles; empty/below-minGenes/maxGap-split/multi-pair edge cases; MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer + Wikipedia; deviations None.
- [[telomere-analysis]] ‚Äî chromosome telomere family anchor (fifth Chromosome-analysis unit): telomere repeat detection + length estimation ‚Äî 3‚Ä≤ end forward TTAGGG / 5‚Ä≤ end reverse-complement CCCTAA (6-bp vertebrate unit, Meyne 1989), configurable 70%-per-window purity so imperfect repeats accepted (5/6 for 6-bp, 5/7 for Arabidopsis TTTAGGG; divergent TTAGGA‚Üí0.833), purity‚àà[0,1] tracked with length; length direct from run or qPCR T/S ratio (Cawthon 2002) EstimatedLength=referenceLength√ó(tsRatio/referenceRatio); IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&length<criticalLength)OR empty; criticalLength 3000 / minTelomereLength 500 / searchLength(truncates) / referenceLength 7000 configurable defaults not biological constants; Wikipedia/Meyne/Cawthon/Blackburn-Gall sources; deviations None. Sibling of [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics common-interval / conserved-cluster unit: a conserved gene cluster = a gene-label SET contiguous in EVERY genome (order- and strand-free inside the window), the common-interval model (Uno & Yagiura 2000, Heber & Stoye 2001 k-permutation O(kn+z), Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 unifying view, Didier et al. 2013 sequences-with-duplicates/paralogs); interval size ‚â•2 (singletons excluded), whole set (1..n) trivially common, meaningful only for K‚â•2; Seqeron does the strict O(n¬≤¬∑K) check with minClusterSize filter; strict gap-free model ‚Äî maxGap retained for API/MCP back-compat only and does NOT relax it, gene-teams gapped extension (Bergeron 2002) not implemented; golden vector Id‚Çá vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) ‚Üí {1,2}/{1,2,3}/{3,4,5,6}/{4,5}/{4,5,6}/{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, duplicates T/S ‚Üí {1,2,3,4}; order-free sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; deviations None.
- [[average-nucleotide-identity]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics ANI family anchor (first COMPGEN unit): the ANIb genome-similarity metric (Goris 2007) that operationalizes the prokaryotic species boundary (ANI‚âà95%‚Üî70% DDH) ‚Äî fragment query into 1020 nt pieces, best-match place each against the reference (`CalculateAni`), keep fragments >30% identity over ‚â•70% alignable (both recalculated over the query-fragment length), average the qualifying per-fragment identities; gapped Smith-Waterman placement recovers indels (`gapped:true`), reciprocal/symmetric ANI = mean of both directions (`CalculateReciprocalAni`, order-independent); null/empty‚Üí0, non-positive fragmentLength throws; engine decision = SequenceAligner.LocalAlign (full DP, BLAST DNA scoring) not NCBI-BLASTN, indel handling correct; sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] in the COMPGEN family; deviations None.
- [[dot-plot-word-match]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics visual pairwise-comparison unit (`COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001`): the word-match / k-tuple dot matrix (Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 ‚Üí EMBOSS `dottup`) ‚Äî dot at (x,y) iff the length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches the word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences via suffix tree), diagonals = similarity / main diagonal = self-comparison / repeats = extra diagonals / indels break the diagonal; `wordSize` (EMBOSS default 10) noise-vs-sensitivity trade-off (longer=less noise/less sensitive), `stepSize` x-subsampling; exact-match `dottup` not scored `dotmatcher`; AGCGT/AT k=1‚Üí{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4‚Üí{(0,0),(0,4),(1,1),(2,2),(3,3),(4,0),(4,4)}, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjoint‚Üíno dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize throws; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics ortholog & in-paralog detection unit (`COMPGEN-ORTHO-001`): orthologs by Reciprocal Best Hits (RBH ‚Äî each gene the other's best hit across two genomes, Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 / Tatusov 1997 / Fitch 1970 speciation-vs-duplication), recent (in-)paralogs by within-genome mutual best hits (Remm 2001); best hit=max-similarity with deterministic tie-break, reciprocity mandatory (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog = the guarded defect), ‚â•50% coverage + min-similarity gates, partial-matching output, empty‚Üíno orthologs / single-gene‚Üíno paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking (reciprocity/coverage/threshold source-backed); shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, the core/shared-gene sub-unit of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]]; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics signed-permutation / breakpoint rearrangement-detection unit (`COMPGEN-REARR-001` + `COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001`): the Hannenhalli‚ÄìPevzner/Bafna‚ÄìPevzner theory ‚Äî signed permutation (strand=sign), extended `(0,‚Ä¶,n+1)` (endpoints=telomeres), breakpoint = consecutive pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(‚àíy,‚àíx)` survives in Œ≤, `b(Œ±)` count = `d_BP=n‚àísim(common adjacencies)`, reversal-distance lower bound `d‚â•b/2`; `ClassifyRearrangement` ‚Üí Inversion (reversal = sign-flip + local reverse) vs Transposition (block move preserving orientation), Translocation/Deletion/Insertion/Duplication "Not implemented" (single permutation can't express them); Hunter `(‚àí2,‚àí3,+1,+6,‚àí5,‚àí4)`‚Üíb=6/d‚â•3, identity‚Üí0, single-inversion `(+1,‚àí4,‚àí3,‚àí2,+5)`‚Üíb=2 oracles; `b‚àà[0,n+1]` invariant; the signed-permutation `alternative_to` the block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]], sibling of ANI/ortholog/clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics end-to-end pipeline (`CompareGenomes`): partitions each genome's genes into core (conserved = RBH ortholog pairs, Tettelin 2005 pan-genome) vs dispensable (genome-specific = the rest), reports Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in MCScanX syntenic blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped ‚â§1; symmetric partition, empty‚Üíall-0; orchestrates RBH ortholog detection (COMPGEN-RBH-001) + synteny (COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001); sibling of [[average-nucleotide-identity]] & [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]]; two source-backed assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate, MCScanX ‚â•5-anchor block threshold ‚Üí OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] ‚Äî protein-disorder family MoRF unit (DISORDER-MORF-001, second DISORDER-* unit): Molecular Recognition Feature prediction by the "dip within disorder" heuristic (Oldfield 2005 / Cheng-Oldfield PMC2570644 / Mohan 2006) ‚Äî a short ordered run (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10‚Äì70 flanked on both sides by disorder (score ‚â•0.5) = one MoRF; 0.5 order/disorder threshold, Œ±/Œ≤/Œπ bound-state sub-types (Mohan 2006), MoRF score‚àà[0,1] rising with dip depth; terminal dip / fully-ordered / fully-disordered / out-of-band ‚Üí none; TOP-IDP normalized `(raw+0.884)/1.871` per-residue score from `PredictDisorder`; one assumption = exact flank-length params paywalled ‚Üí qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]; deviations None.
- [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] ‚Äî protein disorder / features family anchor (first DISORDER-* unit, DISORDER-LC-001): the SEG algorithm (Wootton & Federhen 1993/1996) partitioning a protein into low-/high-complexity segments; complexity = Shannon entropy `H=‚àíŒ£p·µ¢log‚ÇÇp·µ¢` bits/residue (max log‚ÇÇ20‚âà4.322), two-stage scan with W=12 trigger window / K1=2.2 trigger cutoff / K2=2.5 extension cutoff (NCBI `blast_seg.c` defaults); homopolymer H=0 triggers, 12-distinct H‚âà3.585>K2 no segment; X-rich/X-Y-rich label + greedy single-residue extension are flagged repository extensions not moving boundaries; distinct from [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|intrinsic-disorder prediction]] (TOP-IDP) and the genomic-DNA [[repetitive-element-detection]] low-complexity counterpart.
- [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] ‚Äî protein-disorder family shared anchor (DISORDER-PRED-001 + DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 + DISORDER-REGION-001): the TOP-IDP `PredictDisorder` sliding-window intrinsic-disorder predictor (Campen 2008) that [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] + disordered-region detection sit on; also hosts the region-detection layer (contiguous runs ‚â• minRegionLength, default RegionType classification proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich > 0.25 + Long/Standard IDR, opt-in MobiDB-lite flavor scheme); per-residue S·µ¢=mean over window of min-max-normalized TOP-IDP `(p‚àí(‚àí0.884))/1.871 ‚àà [0,1]`, disordered when S·µ¢‚â•0.542 (max-likelihood cutoff), default window 21 (edge-clipped) / minRegionLength 5; Dunker 2001 disorder{A,R,G,Q,S,P,E,K}/order{W,C,F,I,Y,V,L,N}/ambiguous{D,H,M,T} sets + Kyte-Doolittle `CalculateHydropathy`; W30‚Üí0.0/P30‚Üí1.0/E30‚Üí0.866 oracles, null/empty‚Üíempty, non-canonical skipped (all-unknown window‚Üí0.0), case-insensitive, O(n¬∑w); also anchors the raw per-residue propensity primitives (DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001: `GetDisorderPropensity` returns the RAW un-normalized Table-2 value, unknown‚Üí0.0, + the two public Dunker sets); assumptions None (params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic not competitive with IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite; distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]].
- [[aneuploidy-detection]] ‚Äî chromosome copy-number/ploidy family anchor (first Chromosome-analysis unit): abnormal chromosome count from read depth ‚Äî per-bin CN=round(2^log2(depth/median)√ó2) clamped [0,10], whole-chromosome call needs dominant CN across ‚â•80% of bins (mosaicism tolerance), confidence=1‚àímin(1,|CN/2‚àí2^logRatio|)=1.0 at integer-CN ratios; nullisomy..pentasomy terminology; Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosomes-not-special-cased + partial-aneuploidy-needs-80%-bins limitations.
- [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] ‚Äî epigenetics family bisulfite-sequencing unit (second EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-BISULF-001): base-level DNA-methylation calling from sodium-bisulfite reads ‚Äî distinct from the age clock (it *produces* the Œ≤-values a clock consumes). Three deterministic ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: (1) `SimulateBisulfiteConversion` ‚Äî single-strand per-base Frommer 1992 rule (unprotected C‚ÜíT, protected 5mC stays C, non-C unchanged, case preserved, ACGTCGAA{1}‚ÜíACGTTGAA); (2) `CalculateMethylationFromBisulfite` ‚Äî reuses `FindCpGSites`, Bismark C=methylated/T=unmethylated tally, level = meth/(meth+unmeth)‚àà[0,1], zero-coverage sites excluded (ACGTACGT reads‚Üí0.5&0.0); (3) `GenerateMethylationProfile` ‚Äî Schultz 2012 per-context weighted level Œ£(level¬∑coverage)/Œ£coverage (0.25‚âÝunweighted 0.5), zero-total-coverage falls back to unweighted mean; CpG needs C+G, neither-C-nor-T call ignored, past-reference ignored; research-grade, no CHG/CHH calling / no complement merge / no non-conversion-rate correction; sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]; deviations None.
- [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] ‚Äî epigenetics family anchor (first EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-AGE-001): DNAm ("epigenetic") age from methylation Œ≤-values via the Horvath 2013 multi-tissue clock ‚Äî two-stage model, linear predictor `Y = intercept + Œ£ coef_i¬∑Œ≤_i` over 353 elastic-net-selected clock CpGs (transformed-age units), then the two-branch inverse calibration `anti.trafo` (adult.age=20): `21¬∑exp(Y)‚àí1` for Y<0 (exponential), `21¬∑Y+20` for Y‚â•0 (linear), continuous at (0,20)=age 20; embedded intercept 0.695507258 + 353 `CoefficientTraining` weights cross-verified byte-identical; invariants Y=0‚Üí20 / CpGs-absent-ignored / empty-map‚ÜíF‚Åª¬π(intercept); null‚ÜíArgumentNullException, empty coefficients‚ÜíArgumentException; anti.trafo oracles (0‚Üí20, 1‚Üí41, ‚àí1‚Üí6.7254682646, ‚àí2.5‚Üí0.7237849711) + Y=0.684247258‚Üí34.369192418; scope = multi-tissue only (algorithm doc later extends to Horvath-2018 skin&blood 391-CpG + Levine-2018 PhenoAge 513-CpG no-transform); no BMIQ input normalisation (research-grade); sibling [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] (produces the Œ≤-values); third Epigenetics sibling [[chromatin-state-prediction]] (histone-mark axis).
- [[cpg-island-detection]] ‚Äî epigenetics family CpG site & island unit (fourth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CPG-001): sequence-only CpG dinucleotide detection (no methylation state ‚Äî distinct from all siblings). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `FindCpGSites` (linear scan, 0-based C position, `CGCG`‚Üí2 sites, reused by [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]); `CalculateCpGObservedExpected` (Gardiner-Garden O/E=CpG/((C¬∑G)/L), div-by-zero guard‚Üí0, oracles CGCG√ó 2.0/ACGTCGACG 3.0/ACGT 4.0/AT-only 0); `FindCpGIslands` (sliding-window merge, default ‚â•200bp/GC‚â•0.5/O-E‚â•0.6 inclusive, 0-based inclusive-Start/exclusive-End tuple, 400bp CGCG‚Üí1 island, O(n¬∑w)); GpC‚âÝCpG, case-insensitive; Takai-Jones 2002 stricter (‚â•500/55%/0.65) + Saxonov 2006 alt-expected not preset (custom args); Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 + Takai-Jones + Saxonov + Wikipedia; assumptions None. Siblings [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]/[[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]].
- [[chromatin-state-prediction]] ‚Äî epigenetics family chromatin-state / histone-mark unit (third EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CHROM-001): ChromHMM-style (Ernst & Kellis 2012) annotation of a locus from the *combination of present histone marks* ‚Äî distinct from the methylation siblings (operates on histone ChIP-seq signals, not DNA methylation). Binary present/absent mark model (ChromHMM binarizes then learns; state = function of the SET of present marks, magnitude beyond the call irrelevant = binary invariance); `PredictChromatinState` takes the six Roadmap 18-state marks {H3K4me3, H3K4me1, H3K27ac, H3K36me3, H3K27me3, H3K9me3} as [0,1] signals, calls present > threshold (default 0.5), maps pattern ‚Üí ActivePromoter(TssA, H3K4me3¬±H3K27ac)/ActiveEnhancer(H3K4me1+H3K27ac)/WeakEnhancer(H3K4me1 no H3K27ac)/Transcribed(Tx, H3K36me3)/Repressed(ReprPC, H3K27me3)/Heterochromatin(Het, H3K9me3)/BivalentPromoter(TssBiv, H3K4me3+H3K27me3)/BivalentEnhancer(EnhBiv, H3K4me1+H3K27me3)/LowSignal(Quies, none); two combinatorial rules ‚Äî bivalency is a state not a contradiction, promoter(H3K4me3) dominates enhancer(H3K4me1); companions `AnnotateHistoneModifications` (per-mark region label) + `FindAccessibleRegions` (ATAC-like contiguous-merge + minWidth); research-grade ‚Äî state-assignment logic source-backed, NOT a trained HMM (no LearnModel/Poisson binarization/spatial context); two assumptions (0.5 threshold, single-locus precedence); sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] & [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]; no contradictions.
- [[differentially-methylated-regions]] ‚Äî epigenetics family DMR-detection unit (fifth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-DMR-001): methylKit (Akalin 2012) two-sample tiling-window + Fisher's-exact-test model ‚Äî *compares* methylation between two samples (distinct from the single-sample siblings), consuming the per-CpG C/(C+T) Œ≤-values [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] produces over the CpGs [[cpg-island-detection]] locates. Fixed tiles (`win.size=1000/step.size=1000/cov.bases=0`, `tileMethylCounts`), meth.diff=group2%‚àígroup1% (percentage points), per-window pooled 2√ó2 methylated/unmethylated counts ‚Üí Fisher's exact (one sample per group; replicates‚Üílogistic regression out of scope), hypergeometric single-table p `(a+b)!(c+d)!(a+c)!(b+d)!/(a!b!c!d!n!)` + two-sided ‚â§-observed sum; report q<0.01 AND |meth.diff|>25 strict (`getMethylDiff`): hyper meth.diff>+25 / hypo <‚àí25; empty‚Üíno DMRs, zero-coverage group / zero marginal‚Üíp=1.0, |meth.diff|=25‚Üíexcluded; oracles Fisher a=1/b=9/c=11/d=3‚Üí‚âà0.001346076, hyper window g1=0.0/g2=1.0‚Üí+100/p‚âà0; two evidence-backed assumptions (per-window pooling, numC/numT=round(level√ócoverage)); research-grade (no logistic path/SLIM/overlapping tiles); siblings [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]]; no contradictions.
- [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] ‚Äî Analysis alignment-free pairwise-similarity unit (`GENOMIC-SIMILARITY-001`, `GenomicAnalyzer.CalculateSimilarity`): Jaccard index of the two sequences' distinct k-mer sets (Jaccard 1901 `|A‚à©B|/|A‚à™B|` over HashSet k-mer sets, Ondov 2016 *Mash* fraction-of-shared-k-mers), exact (no MinHash sketch) J√ó100 in `[0,100]`, O(n+m); INV symmetry / identical‚Üí100 / disjoint‚Üí0 / distinct-set (repeats once); default k=5, empty-union‚Üí0 (ASM-1 convention), √ó100 scaling; k=3 oracles 80/(100/3)/100/0; `alternative_to` positional [[alignment-statistics]], the 5-mer-Jaccard metric behind [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] and the exact-set basis Mash sketches for [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; limitations = exact-match/composition-only; deviations None.
- [[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] ‚Äî K-mer family alignment-free word-frequency **distance** unit (`KMER-DIST-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.KmerDistance`): Euclidean (L2) distance between two sequences' normalized k-mer **frequency** vectors `f_s(w)=count/(L‚àík+1)` over the union of observed k-mers (absent word‚Üí0 component), exact/O(n+m); Zielezinski 2017 word-vector model + Lau 2022 frequency normalization + Vinga-Almeida 2003 4^k-vector + Boden 2014 relative-frequency Euclidean; INV d(x,x)=0 / symmetric / ‚â•0 / disjoint-single-kmer‚Üí‚àö2; ‚àö0.11‚âà0.3316624790 (ATGTGTG/CATGTG k=3) + ‚àö0.125 (AAAA/AAAT k=1) oracles; case-insensitive (ASM-01) + empty/L<k‚Üízero-vector (ASM-02); count-based/Manhattan/Canberra/Chebyshev/cosine/D2/spaced-word not implemented, deviations None; `alternative_to` the presence/absence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] (this captures abundance), shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]] ‚Äî K-mer family async count unit (`KMER-ASYNC-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersAsync`): the cooperatively cancelable, progress-reporting thread-pool wrapper over synchronous `CountKmers` ‚Äî numeric result identical to the sync reference (counts fixed by the k-mer formula `L ‚àí k + 1`, n·µè possible), so the distinctive validated content is *execution* not arithmetic: the .NET cancellation contract (`ThrowIfCancellationRequested`‚ÜíOperationCanceledException + Canceled state, pre-start `Task.Run(func,token)` cancellation, awaiting a canceled task throws) + `IProgress<double>` 0‚Üí1.0; INV Œ£counts=L‚àík+1 / empty¬∑k>L‚Üíempty dict / k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException via awaited task; uppercased (case-insensitive) + alphabet-agnostic (IUPAC N counted literally); ATGG‚Üí{ATG:1,TGG:1} + GTAGAGCTGT oracles; one assumption = numeric contract identical to sync (non-correctness-affecting); single-thread offload (not parallelized), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; wraps sync KMER-COUNT-001 (not yet ingested); record [[kmer-async-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-generation]] ‚Äî K-mer family *space-enumeration* unit (`KMER-GENERATE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.GenerateAllKmers`): exhaustive enumeration of ALL possible k-mers of length `k` over an alphabet ‚Äî the complete k-mer universe `Œ£^k` of size `n^k` (4^k for DNA), depends only on `k`+alphabet not on any sequence; DISTINCT from counting (produces the full n^k word set / address space, siblings extract observed substrings + counts); k-fold Cartesian product `itertools.product(Œ£,repeat=k)`, lazy recursive prefix-extension, odometer emission ‚Üí lexicographic for a sorted alphabet; INV n^k count / all-distinct-set / length-k / sorted‚Üílexicographic; k=1‚Üí{A,C,G,T}, k=2‚Üí16 (AA..TT), k=3‚Üí64, protein 20^2=400, single-letter 1^4=1 oracles; k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty alphabet‚ÜíArgumentException, unsorted‚Üípositional order, verbatim/no-dedup; O(k¬∑n^k) time/O(k) lazy space, suffix-tree N/A (generates not searches); shares the "ACGT"-default + k‚â§0-throws API contract with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] but NOT the `CountKmers` primitive; supplies the index space for [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]]/[[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]]; deviations None; record [[kmer-generate-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-positions]] ‚Äî K-mer family *occurrence-index* unit (`KMER-POSITIONS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindKmerPositions`): the ascending 0-based positions where a given k-mer occurs in a sequence ‚Äî *where*, not *how many* (the inverse index to the counting units) ‚Äî solving the exact Pattern Matching Problem `Occ(P,T)={i‚àà[0,L‚àík]:T[i..i+k)=P}` with all overlapping starts reported; INV-01..04 (match predicate / ascending / count=overlap-occurrences / range `[0,L‚àík]`, empty when k>L); case-insensitive upper-casing (sibling `CountKmers`), unrestricted-text alphabet, null/empty & k>L & absent ‚Üí empty (no throw), whole-seq‚Üí`[0]`; `ATAT`/`GATATATGCATATACTT`‚Üí`[1,3,9]` + `AA`/`AAAA`‚Üí`[0,1,2]` oracles; O(L¬∑k) naive span scan, suffix-tree evaluated-not-used (unordered leaves, single-query no amortization); three API-shape assumptions (0-based, case-fold, empty-not-throw), deviations None; the single-pattern K-mer sibling of multi-pattern [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the counting siblings [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-positions-001-evidence]].
- [[both-strand-kmer-counting]] ‚Äî K-mer family strand-aware count unit (`KMER-BOTH-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersBothStrands`): the ADDITIVE / kPAL-"balance" both-strand profile `count[w] = forward[w] + forward[RC(w)]` (count k-mers of S and of RC(S), sum per key), grounded in inversion symmetry (Shporer 2016) + kPAL balance (Anvar 2014); distinct from ‚Äî and does NOT implement ‚Äî the canonical-collapsing convention (lexicographically-smaller of {w,RC(w)} as one key, Jellyfish `-C` / Mash); INV Œ£count=2¬∑(L‚àík+1) / count[w]=count[RC(w)] strand-symmetric / palindrome RC(w)=w‚Üícount doubled on one key; two linear passes O(n¬∑k), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; case-insensitive/IUPAC-complemented, empty¬∑k>L‚Üíempty dict, k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException (inherited from `CountKmers`); ATGGC k=2‚Üí{AT:2,TG:1,GG:1,GC:2,CC:1,CA:1} + ACGT‚Üí{AC:2,CG:2,GT:2} + AAA‚Üí{AA:2,TT:2} oracles; built on the same sync `CountKmers` primitive as [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; two API-shape assumptions, deviations None; record [[kmer-both-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-statistics]] ‚Äî K-mer family *summary-statistics* unit (`KMER-STATS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.AnalyzeKmers`): a companion summary layer over the shared `CountKmers` multiset that reduces the count profile to `KmerStatistics` {TotalKmers=L‚àík+1=Œ£counts, UniqueKmers=**distinct** count, MaxCount, MinCount, AverageCount=total/distinct (rounded 2dp), Entropy=Shannon **k-entropy** `‚àíŒ£ p(Œ±)log‚ÇÇp(Œ±)`, `p=mult/(L‚àík+1)`, bits}; the one distinct piece of content is the k-entropy (Manca 2021 + Entropy‚ÄìRank Ratio, corroborated by Wikipedia/BioInfoLogics count tables); GOTCHA `UniqueKmers` = distinct count NOT the count==1 singletons (that is KMER-UNIQUE-001); INV Total=Œ£counts / Unique=distinct(CountKmers) / homopolymer‚ÜíH0,max=min=total / all-distinct‚ÜíH log‚ÇÇD,max=min=1 / k>L¬∑empty‚Üíall-zero; GTAGAGCTGT k=1 (10/4/4/1/2.5/1.8464) + k=3 (8/8/1/1/log‚ÇÇ8=3.0) + ATCGATCAC k=3 (7/6/2/1/2.5216) + AAAA k=2 (3/1/3/3/0) oracles; case-insensitive, k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException; two presentation-only assumptions (AverageCount 2dp, Entropy unrounded); shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]], distinct from generation/positions/distance siblings; deviations None; record [[kmer-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]] ‚Äî K-mer family *frequency-filtering* unit (`KMER-UNIQUE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`): selects k-mers by their per-k-mer **Count** (overlapping occurrences, Compeau & Pevzner `Count(Text,Pattern)`) at opposite ends of the frequency distribution ‚Äî `FindUniqueKmers` = the `Count==1` **singletons**, `FindKmersWithMinCount` = the `Count‚â•minCount` **recurrent** k-mers ordered by count desc; total/distinct/unique terminology (BioInfoLogics: unique = "appear only once"; Wikipedia L‚àík+1 total); GOTCHA "unique"=singleton set here ‚âÝ [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `UniqueKmers`=distinct count (ATCGATCAC k=3 ‚Üí 5 unique vs 6 distinct, ATC=2 excluded); oracles ATCGATCAC k=3‚Üí{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC}, AGAT k=2‚Üí{AG,GA,AT}, ACGTACGT k=4 FindKmersWithMinCount(‚Ä¶,2)‚Üí{(ACGT,2)}/(‚Ä¶,1)‚Üíall-4-count-desc/FindUniqueKmers‚Üí{CGTA,GTAC,TACG}, AAAAA k=3‚Üí‚àÖ; case-insensitive, k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty¬∑k>L‚Üíempty; two assumptions (minCount‚â§1‚Üíall distinct count-desc; upper-casing), deviations None; filters the shared `CountKmers` multiset like [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]].
- [[longest-common-substring]] ‚Äî Sequence-Comparison longest-common-substring / common-region-detection unit (`GENOMIC-COMMON-001`): the maximal *contiguous* substring shared by two strings (distinct from the gapped longest common *subsequence*) via a generalized suffix tree (LCS = deepest internal node whose subtree holds leaves from both strings, Œò(n+m) build + DFS, Gusfield 1997); `FindLongestCommonRegion` (0-based positions in both) + `FindCommonRegions(minLength)` (all distinct shared runs ‚â• minLength), None=empty/len 0/pos ‚àí1, identical‚Üíwhole seq at 0/0; documented deterministic first-found-in-`other` tie-break (CACAGAG/TACATAGAT ties ACA vs AGA ‚Üí ACA); Wikipedia + GeeksforGeeks sources, shares the suffix-tree exact-match engine with [[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[longest-repeated-substring]] ‚Äî Repeat-Analysis LRS + repeat-enumeration unit (`GENOMIC-REPEAT-001`): the longest substring recurring within *one* DNA sequence (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindLongestRepeat`) + all distinct substrings occurring ‚â•2√ó with length ‚â• minLength (`FindRepeats`), both via the *single-string* suffix tree's deepest internal node with ‚â•2 leaves (string depth = repeat length; CMU ¬ß2.1 / Wikipedia / GeeksforGeeks App-3 / Gusfield 5.4); overlaps counted, no-repeat/empty‚Üí`RepeatInfo.None`, `minLength‚â§0`‚Üí`max(1,minLength)`, ACGT-only, no reverse-complement/maximal-repeat classification; FindRepeats via sorted-suffix adjacent-LCP *every-prefix* enumeration (O(n¬≤), FINDINGS_REGISTER short-prefix fix); ATCGATCGA‚ÜíATCGA{0,4}, AAAAAAAAAA‚ÜíAAAAAAAAA{0,1}, ATATATA‚ÜíATATA{0,2}, ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3‚Üí8-substring oracles; the *single-string* sibling of [[longest-common-substring]], distinct from the tandem/inverted [[repetitive-element-detection]] anchor; tie-break + ascending-positions assumptions, deviations None.
- [[open-reading-frame-detection]] ‚Äî Analysis ORF-detection unit (`GENOMIC-ORF-001`): six-frame ATG‚Üífirst-in-frame-stop enumeration (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindOpenReadingFrames`), standard code (start ATG / stops TAA-TAG-TGA), reported span **includes** the stop (Length%3==0) while the translated protein **excludes** it; THE correctness rule = every in-frame ATG reaching a stop reported, so **nested ORFs sharing a stop** both returned (Rosalind `MGMTPRLGLESLLE`/`MTPRLGLESLLE`), ATG-with-no-stop‚Üínone; `minLength` in **nucleotides** inclusive (default 100), 0-based Position, Frame 1‚Äì3 + IsReverseComplement, INV-01..05 (starts ATG / ends stop / len%3==0 / ‚â•minLength / six-frame), O(n¬≤) worst / O(n) typical; Rosalind_99‚Üí4 distinct proteins + ATGAAAAAATAA‚ÜíMKK oracles; Rosalind + Wikipedia + NCBI ORFfinder + transl_table=1 sources; deviations None (one fixed greedy bug); deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to annotation `GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs` (ANNOT-ORF-001: ATG/GTG/TTG, aa-length, strand/start flags) or `Translator.FindOrfs` (genetic-code-parameterized); coding potential is a separate step ([[coding-potential-hexamer-score]]).
- [[known-motif-search]] ‚Äî Motif-Analysis known-motif-search anchor (`GENOMIC-MOTIFS-001`): multi-pattern **exact** substring matching of a caller-supplied set of known query motifs (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif`) ‚Äî the "you know what you're looking for" exact-equality baseline, distinct from motif *discovery* and *degenerate* (IUPAC/PROSITE/PWM) matching; THE correctness rule = all **overlapping** occurrences reported (AAA in AAAAA‚Üí{0,1,2}, per Gusfield/Biopython `count_overlap` 3-not-2); 0-based sorted positions, per-motif position lists with absent motifs omitted, upper-cased result keys, empty/whitespace motif‚Üíno entry (`Array.Empty<int>()`); EcoRI GAATTC‚Üí{0,9} + `{ACGT,AA,TTT}` in ACGTACGTAA oracles; Tufts/Gusfield + Biopython `Seq.search` + Wikipedia "Restriction site" sources; shares exact-all-occurrences semantics with [[longest-common-substring]]/[[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[alpha-diversity]] ‚Äî Metagenomics diversity family anchor (first META-* unit, META-ALPHA-001): within-sample diversity indices from one taxon‚Üíabundance map (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateAlphaDiversity` ‚Üí `AlphaDiversity` record) ‚Äî observed richness S_obs, Shannon H=‚àíŒ£p·µ¢ln(p·µ¢) in nats, Simpson concentration Œª=Œ£p·µ¢¬≤, inverse Simpson 1/Œª (Hill order-2 effective species), Pielou evenness J=H/ln(S) for S>1 else 0, Chao1 S_obs+f‚ÇÅ¬≤/(2f‚ÇÇ) (f‚ÇÇ=0‚Üíbias-corrected S_obs+f‚ÇÅ(f‚ÇÅ‚àí1)/2, non-integer/proportional‚ÜíS_obs); Whittaker 1960 Œ±/Œ≤/Œ≥ framework, Shannon 1948/Simpson 1949/Hill 1973/Chao 1984/Pielou 1966; counts-or-proportions internally normalized, non-positive filtered, O(n); empty/null‚Üíall-0, single species‚ÜíH0/Œª1/J0; one accepted deviation = Chao1 count-vs-proportion gate; between-sample [[beta-diversity]] its sibling; deviations else None.
